class=\"col-sm-12 col-md-8\">\n                                <div class=\"text-content\">\n                                    <div class=\"lead text-uppercase\">Now Through May 2</div>\n                                    <h2><a href=\"/AOTR2017Feature\">Art of the Real</a></h2>\n                                    <div class=\"summary\">\n                                        A survey of the most vital and innovative voices in nonfiction and hybrid filmmaking, this year's edition features established figures such as Ignacio Agüero, Jem Cohen, and the late Michael Glawogger alongside up-and-comers Theo Anthony and Salomé Jashi, as well as a tribute to the late Brazilian filmmaker Andrea Tonacci.\n                                    </div>\n                                </div>\n   \n\n            <div class=\"col-sm-12 col-md-6 home-feature home-feature-secondary module\" data-post-id=\"139080\">\n\n                <div class=\"snippet related-post content-box class=\"snippet-image\" src=\"https://www.filmlinc.org/wp-content/uploads/2017/02/slackbay-480x270-c-default.jpg\">\n                        </a>\n                                            </div>\n\n\n\n                    <div class=\"related-text\">\n\n                        <div class=\"snippet-type text-uppercase\">Now Playing</div>\n                        <h3 class=\"snippet-title\"><a href=\"/SlackBayFeature\">Slack Bay</a></h3>\n                                                    <div class=\"summary\">\n                                <br>Juliette Binoche, Fabrice Luchini, and Valeria Bruni Tedeschi costar in this surreal, weirdly captivating mix of slapstick comedy and oddball detective story, the latest foray into farce from former enfant terrible Bruno Dumont. A Kino Lorber release.\n                            </div>\n                                                <a href=\"/SlackBayFeature\" class=\"cta snippet-cta arrow text-uppercase\">Get Tickets\n                            <i class=\"fa fa-chevron-right\"></i>\n                        </a>\n                    </div>\n\n                </div>\n\n            </div>\n            \n        \n        \n                                    \n        \n\n            <div class=\"col-sm-12 col-md-6 home-feature home-feature-secondary module\" data-post-id=\"140799\">\n\n                <div class=\"snippet related-post content-box js-match-height\" data-mh=\"secondary-feature-text\" style=\"\">\n\n                    <div class=\"inner\">\n                        <a href=\"https://www.filmlinc.org/PrintScreenBoucherFeature\">\n                            <img class=\"snippet-image\" src=\"https://www.filmlinc.org/wp-content/uploads/2017/03/leboucher-1-480x270-c-default.jpg\">\n                        </a>\n                                            </div>\n\n\n\n                    <div class=\"related-text\">\n\n                        <div class=\"snippet-type text-uppercase\">April 25 · Tickets on sale now!</div>\n                        <h3 class=\"snippet-title\"><a href=\"https://www.filmlinc.org/PrintScreenBoucherFeature\">Print Screen: Katie Kitamura and <em>Le Boucher</em></a></h3>\n                                                    <div class=\"summary\">\n                                Kitamura’s latest, <em>A Separation </em>, is a suspenseful account of intimacy and infidelity, unfolding in a remote Greek Village. To pair with her acclaimed new work, Kitamura has chosen Claude Chabrol’s seminal relationship thriller <em>Le Boucher</em>.\n                            </div>\n
